(Paris) The Bank of France today increased the discount rate from 5% to 6%. This is the government's first measure to protect the franc and prevent its depreciation. The bank had increased the discount rate from 3.5% to 5% on March 28. (6th, Guomin Telegraph)

US-French Commercial Treaty Signed

Trade Reciprocity to Take Effect Next Month

(Washington) The State Department announced today that the US-French reciprocal commercial treaty has been signed and will take effect on June 15. The treaty stipulates most-favored-nation treatment, including France increasing import quotas for American goods and the United States reducing import taxes on certain French items. The treaty is the result of negotiations that began a year ago and is the thirteenth commercial treaty signed by the United States, second in importance only to the US-Canada commercial treaty. It will not only be applied to France but also to French colonies, territories, and protectorates, with the exception of Morocco. The treaty can be terminated by either country giving six months' notice after January 1, 1937. (6th, Reuters Telegraph)

(Paris) The commercial treaty between the United States and France was signed in Washington yesterday and will take effect on June 15 of this year and expire on July 1 of next year. Its provisions have not yet been made public, but it is only known that the import tax rates on the goods with the most trade between the two countries, such as French wine and lace, and American fruits and automobiles, will be reduced. In addition, both sides will enjoy most-favored-nation treatment. This is the most important of the commercial treaties that the United States has signed with European countries since the United States Reciprocal Trade Agreements Act was promulgated in March 1934. (7th, Havas Telegraph)

German Large Airship Hindenburg Flies to the United States

Cooperation with American Aviation for North Atlantic Trial Flight

Friedrichshafen The German largest new airship Hindenburg flew from here to Lakehurst, New Jersey, in the United States at 9:30 PM this afternoon. This is the starting point for testing whether it is possible to establish regular commercial aviation services on the North Atlantic. The US authorities are cooperating and allowing the airship to use the naval base at Lakehurst. It is reported that the Hindenburg recently completed its first flight on the South Atlantic, flying from Lake Constance in Germany to Brazil. (6th, Reuters Telegraph)

Hindenburg Airship The latest German large airship "Hindenburg" departed at 9:30 PM tonight and flew to Lakehurst, New Jersey, in the United States. It has begun transporting mail, cargo, and passengers on the North Atlantic. This time, there are 49 passengers, including 7 women and 7 journalists. Miller, the European bureau manager of the Associated Press, is also on board. The designer of the airship, Dr. Eckener, and Lieutenant Commander Lehmann are jointly responsible for driving. In addition, there are 50 staff members. The airship took off from the Friedrichshafen airfield in Germany in the moonlight. The airfield played military music and illuminated with electric torches. It is said that if the weather does not change, after arriving at Lakehurst, it will fly over the cities of New York, Washington, and Baltimore. Lehmann told Miller that the current weather report is very good, but he did not hope to complete the trip quickly. (6th, Guomin Telegraph)

Mrs. Mollison Sets New Solo Flight Record

London to Cape Town in Three Days and Six and a Half Hours

Cape Town Mrs. Mollison arrived here safely at 4:31 PM today (local time), setting a new solo flight record from England to Cape Town. Mrs. Mollison completed the entire journey in three days, six hours, and twenty-six minutes, which is eleven hours and nine minutes less than the record held by Air Force Lieutenant Rose. Thousands of people gathered at the airfield to await Mrs. Mollison's arrival. As Mrs. Mollison's plane slowly landed, the crowd shouted, "Success, Amy!" Mrs. Mollison described the scene as extremely frightening when she flew over the Sahara Desert. Mrs. Mollison had scheduled the itinerary, but was delayed in Wolan while waiting for the weather report. Later, because she did not want to arrive at Inowar Point at night, she spent several hours. (7th, Reuters Telegraph)

Algiers Chaotic and Broken

Scattered Troops Attack French Embassy

Algiers After four days in a state of terror, there was still gunfire last night as armed gangs repeatedly attacked the city's shopping district. The area is in a state of utter disarray, as if after a major storm, with only burned, demolished, and looted shops remaining. The streets are littered with debris, and sometimes bodies can be seen. Since law and order has been lost, countless people are taking advantage of this opportunity to vent old grudges. It is estimated that a total of 500 Algerians have been killed in the riots. The British, French, German, and Italian embassies are all unscathed, and these seem to be the only buildings that have not been demolished. A French school was attacked and burned on the second day of the riots. (7th, Reuters Telegraph)

Algiers Several Algerian rebels recently attacked the French embassy with machine guns. The Italian military headquarters dispatched three tanks and 50 Ascari soldiers to suppress the attack, killing several rebels. Several people seeking refuge in the embassy were also hit by stray bullets. The rebels were quickly defeated and retreated. Last night, gunfire was still heard sporadically in various parts of the capital. Today, it has gradually calmed down. (6th, Havas Telegraph)

Italy Will Not Establish a Puppet Monarch in Abyssinia

But Will Appoint Several Puppet Governors

(Rome) Italy's decision on the future status of Abyssinia will not be announced before the League of Nations Council meeting on Monday, and it may not even be announced at the meeting. Italian officials are now keeping silent, only saying that they will respect the treaty rights of Britain and France. Italian officials did not expect the rapid occupation of Addis Ababa by the Italian army and the hasty escape of the Abyssinian Emperor. Many believe that the Abyssinian Emperor's escape is legally equivalent to abdication, so Abyssinia currently does not have a government that Italy can negotiate with. The Abyssinian representative in Geneva does not have credentials and cannot engage in negotiations. Therefore, Italy is now responsible for creating a new government. It is estimated that Abyssinia will be under military rule for a long time. It is not believed here that a puppet monarch will be established, but several governors may be established and given autonomous powers. Gugsa, an Abyssinian chieftain who surrendered to the Italian army at the beginning of the war, will be one of the governors. (7th, Reuters Telegraph)

(Rome) Fascist party leaders have determined a procedure for immediately developing Abyssinia. According to reliable sources, the first step is to appoint the current Italian military commander in Somalia, Graziani, as the military governor, the current commander of the Blackshirt Division in Africa, Starace, as the civil governor, and the current commander of the Italian army in Abyssinia, Badoglio, will be recalled and resume his position as chief of staff of the General Staff. Also, according to a famous banker who told reporters, the Italian government will soon borrow foreign debts from foreign countries to develop Abyssinia. (6th, Guomin Telegraph)

India Withdraws from Ottawa Agreement

Shimla It is reported that the Indian government has issued a notice to immediately terminate the Ottawa Agreement. British Labour Party Proposes in the House of Commons: Continuing Sanctions Against Italy

Sharply Criticizing the Government for Indecision and Delay; Eden Declares Consideration of All Issues

(London) Today, the Labour Party in the House of Commons attacked the government's policies regarding the Italo-Abyssinian dispute and advocated for the continuation of economic and financial sanctions against Italy.

The debate today was initiated by Labour MP Dalton, who stated that the loss of credibility of the League of Nations and the entire collective security system was the responsibility of the British government. He argued that the British government had failed to fulfill the mandate given to it by the voters. On the one hand, the government failed to fulfill its obligations under the League of Nations Covenant, especially Article 16. On the other hand, it encouraged Abyssinia to resist Italy, leading the Abyssinians to believe that the League of Nations would surely provide assistance. However, it allowed Abyssinia to fend for itself without providing any aid. Moreover, not only did it not provide assistance, but it also permitted the continued supply of oil, essential to Italy, thus aiding Italy in destroying the Abyssinian government and profiting from the sale of oil by the Anglo-Iranian (i.e., Persian) Oil Company. Dalton also stated that this was not a matter between a defeated Abyssinia and a victorious Italy, but rather a matter between the entire League of Nations and a country that had been judged as an aggressor. The aggressor, using its overwhelmingly superior weapons, had violated its solemnly concluded treaties against the use of barbaric warfare and had achieved a significant victory under extremely unequal conditions. In this situation, there was no reason to lift the sanctions or recognize Italy's victory. Since sanctions were unanimously imposed on Italy by the League of Nations, the Labour Party advocated that economic and financial sanctions should continue to be enforced.

Liberal Party's Sinclair also stated that the issue between the League of Nations and Italy had not yet been resolved. Abyssinia's defeat at the hands of the aggressor was a great disgrace. Public opinion would not forgive the governments of the countries that created this disgrace, as the responsibility lies not only with the British government.

Chamberlain States: Continuing Sanctions is Indeed Dangerous

Former Foreign Secretary Austen Chamberlain stated that some people hold the view that Britain can accomplish something in the League of Nations, or enable the League of Nations to realize its effectiveness, only if Britain acknowledges that its contributions must lean towards a major power. To hold such a view is to live in a fool's paradise. In his opinion, once a major power has intentionally decided on an act of aggression, even the threat of economic sanctions cannot stop it. For this reason, in the early stages of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, he had calculated the cost and prepared to actively engage with other countries, even to the point of using force. However, now that the situation has changed, continuing sanctions at this time is not only dangerous but also an ineffective policy. Our hope of safeguarding the implementation of the rules of war through the actions of the League of Nations has now failed. However, human success comes from failure. We should make a genuine effort to bring Germany and others back into the League of Nations. The question of whether the League of Nations Covenant needs to be amended so that the Executive Council or the Assembly can act promptly in a dispute, or make decisions before a tragedy unfolds, should be considered. He believed that the government's view of establishing the League of Nations with such local conventions and guarantees was correct.

Eden Explains: Why Not Close the Suez Canal

Foreign Secretary Eden rose to respond, first reporting the news that Dr. Meile, a doctor from the British ambulance team in Addis Ababa, had been shot and seriously injured by a mob in the street and had died. He then spoke about the work of the Indian soldier guard of the British Embassy in Addis Ababa during the serious situation, stating that this guard had saved the lives of many foreigners, not only protecting approximately 2,000 people of 23 nationalities who had taken refuge in the British Embassy but also dispatching detachments to various places to rescue people from danger. All those who requested assistance were answered. The Abyssinian government had thanked the British government for the protection of its embassy by the Indian soldiers. The officer commanding this guard had indeed maintained the inherent highest honor of the Indian army. The Foreign Secretary then responded to the criticism of the government's policies, stating that the situation faced by Britain and other member states of the League of Nations was difficult and disappointing. Britain had consistently held a leading position in this dispute. The sales of British oil had decreased from 13 percent to 4 percent in 1935. Even if sales were completely stopped, what difference would it make to the outcome of this dispute? Among the governments in Geneva, only Britain openly advocated for an oil embargo. Britain was well aware that the weakness of sanctions was their inability to be immediately effective. The only immediately effective sanction would be to prevent Italy from using the Suez Canal. However, this action would inevitably involve military action and ultimately lead to war. Although the opposition party claimed to want to defend the League of Nations with cavalry, infantry, and artillery, in reality, they only wanted to support the League of Nations with threats, insults, and empty talk. It should be understood that Britain cannot close the canal with paper ships. If Britain did not advocate for military sanctions, it was because they were afraid of war and its ultimate consequences. Legally speaking, the canal cannot be closed without the action of the League of Nations. The opposition party should observe the attitude of many governments towards sanctions and be convinced that the League of Nations would certainly pass a resolution to close the canal.

May Experience: The League of Nations Must Decide Its Future

This was hopeless. In the future, it is clear that the League of Nations must proceed as an indispensable international organization in a new world. However, it is also clear that the governments and individual members of the League of Nations, having shouldered responsibility, must carefully consider the results obtained from the experience of the past three months, and the League of Nations must, as a whole, decide on the path of future action. The British government proposed to immediately undertake consideration of the various difficulties arising from this, and therefore will begin discussions with the governments of overseas autonomous territories. We must admit that the League of Nations' actions failed to prevent the outbreak of war before it occurred, nor did they stop the fighting after the war had begun. At most, the League of Nations only made war more difficult and more costly. Therefore, the world and the League of Nations are now faced with terrible problems. Can we foresee that the League of Nations can implement stricter actions than before in the future? Can member states bear greater risks than before? Can the actions of the League of Nations be more preventive than retaliatory? These are just some of the issues we face, and others will not be listed for now. Therefore, the future is difficult and not trivial, but the government will address it with a pragmatic spirit and constructive political skills. The Foreign Secretary did not wish to comment on the policies he would adopt at the League of Nations Executive Council meeting on Monday, stating that under these circumstances, his request for the House of Commons to have faith in him should not be considered unreasonable.

The Foreign Secretary then spoke of the question of asking the German government about peace terms, saying that he hoped the British Ambassador to Germany would be able to submit this question to the German government tomorrow. The Foreign Secretary also responded to Lloyd George's question, saying that the government was well aware that some points had special relations with other governments, but the British government would now submit this question to Germany on its own responsibility. The government's goal in this negotiation remained the same as at the beginning of the negotiation, namely to turn a dangerous period into a period of opportunity. The unilateral cancellation of the Locarno Treaty had shaken the structure of European security. Our work now is to rebuild it. Britain has already made some contributions in the past and now intends to continue this work, feeling that there is nothing more urgent than this. We should not turn a blind eye to the current dangers. Military preparations are now being made everywhere in the world. In fact, several countries seem to disregard all other needs in their national economy and only focus on adding to their military strength. What Britain should do now is to: 1. Implement various peaceful methods to seek the resolution of outstanding issues; 2. Utilize various opportunities to enhance international harmony; 3. Implement the plan to rebuild military strength, as rebuilding military strength has now become an indispensable element in resolving various difficulties, because no matter what the future of the world may be, or what the future of the world organization may be, Britain has its own responsibility, and without military strength as its tool, it cannot effectively fulfill its responsibility in this armed world.

Henderson (son of former Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson) not only supported the proposal to continue sanctions but also advocated for the recall of the British Ambassador to Italy and the expulsion of Italy from the League of Nations.

Churchill Says: We All Feel a Strange Shame

Churchill spoke, sharply criticizing Prime Minister Baldwin, saying that Baldwin had said that he regarded the Italian occupation of Addis Ababa as a strange shame. We all feel a strange shame, but who caused it? Churchill also attacked Baldwin for not participating in the debate, saying that the person in power was not present to respond. He also said that this debate had greatly damaged British affairs, and that continuing the debate would inevitably cause discouragement.

Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs Cranborne responded on behalf of the government, saying that the government had various reasons to be proud of its actions in the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. We sacrificed money and took great risks to uphold the principles we believed in, but because a system failed to be effective, the result was disappointment. We must clean up this position. This cleanup must be thorough to determine whether the League of Nations can be made effective.

The only Communist member of the House of Commons, Gallagher, spoke unceasingly amidst the jeers of government party members until the adjournment, so the Labour Party's motion was not put to a vote. (Reuters, June 6)

Whether to Continue Sanctions Against Italy Becomes a Current Issue for the League of Nations

League of Nations Executive Council to Meet on the 11th; Representatives from Various Countries Will Have Important Contacts

(London) British political circles have recently advocated adopting a "wait-and-see policy" on the Abyssinian issue, believing that Foreign Secretary Eden will certainly attend the League of Nations Executive Council meeting on the 11th of this month, but he should adopt the attitude of the majority of member states. As for the issue of sanctions against Italy, the British House of Commons had originally inclined towards a motion to lift them, but since Léon Blum, leader of the French Orthodox Socialist Party, gave an interview to the Daily Herald, supporting the principle of collective security, Major Attlee, leader of the Labour Party caucus in the British opposition House of Commons, immediately decided to go to Paris at the end of this week to discuss the international situation with the leaders of the French Socialist Party. American Invention: Night-Flying Carrier Pigeons

— Jiang Renjie

The year 1936 has already begun, and what the world often hears is the call for a Second World War, and what newspapers read are the figures of the great powers' armaments. However, one thing is certain, that is, if the Second World War does indeed come, the relationship between science and war will become even closer, and strategy will become more scientific and mechanized. Now, scientists in various countries are already immersed in research. The night-flying carrier pigeons invented by the U.S. Army Signal Corps is a good example.

Military carrier pigeons all fly during the day. If you want to convey military information at night, ordinary military carrier pigeons are useless. After ten years of effort and research, the U.S. Army Signal Corps has actually invented a kind of night-flying carrier pigeon that can safely deliver military information to headquarters or other destinations at a speed of one mile per minute in the darkest night, or on a day with heavy rain, heavy snow, or foggy weather. This group of night flyers is not only the latest invention of the U.S. Army in terms of combat communications, but also a most amazing scientific invention.

Last summer, signal corps stationed at various posts in the United States conducted many experiments, which proved that these carrier pigeons are not only more reliable in night flights but also more stable compared with other types of carrier pigeons. Regardless of whether they are released from airplanes flying at sea or from airplanes flying at high altitudes on land, they can all fly back safely. Usually, they are released from broad plains, dense forests, or dense cities, and they will never get lost or separated.

For example, not long ago, in the Hawaiian Islands, a U.S. territory, the U.S. Army and Navy conducted a combat exercise. At that time, many bomber planes had flown 30 miles from the land, and it was at night. The pilots then tried to release a batch of these newly invented carrier pigeons. This group of birds actually safely carried the information back to their nests 35 minutes later. In actual warfare, the importance of this confidential military information brought back can naturally be imagined. As for the land tests, after being released in dense cities on the American continent, these carrier pigeons can also safely return from a distance of 10 to 15 miles.

Some people must doubt that this is the world of wireless radio, where military information can be transmitted by wireless radio everywhere, and the manufacture of wireless radio is improving day by day, becoming more and more refined. Hasn't the U.S. Army Signal Corps wasted money, spent years of time, and wasted so much effort to invent these carrier pigeons, isn't that a waste of time and extremely foolish? In fact, many military experts are now convinced that in future large-scale military operations, relying on wireless radio for communication will be useless. For example, according to reports, the Italian wireless radio inventor Marconi has already invented a very strong radio column that can emit extremely strong power to airplanes to destroy the electrical machinery on the planes and prevent them from flying. In the midst of war between two countries, both sides of the attack and defense will definitely try to gain an advantage by surprise, and all kinds of unexpected scientific methods will be realized. At this moment, machines that radiate radio columns to interfere with the radio waves emitted by wireless radio, or to deafen wireless radio receivers, have already been invented. This kind of radio column machine can be used at any time in a stronger wireless radio station, or in a large power plant. It can also be used in mobile marching troops. Therefore, when actual war occurs, the effectiveness of wireless radio communication depends entirely on the location of the battlefield, and generally speaking, its effectiveness will inevitably be reduced. That is why you have to rely on carrier pigeons. Because no matter how strong the radio waves that disrupt wireless radio communication are, they have absolutely no effect on carrier pigeons.

This batch of night-flying carrier pigeons was successfully trained in the Monmouth Army Base area of ​​New Jersey, USA. The managing expert is Ross. According to Ross, the way carrier pigeons distinguish direction and choose flight routes is very similar to the way airplane pilots navigate airplanes, but it is mysterious as to how they are able to do so. Ross is a world authority on raising and training pigeons. He said, "It is generally believed that carrier pigeons have a homing instinct. The so-called homing instinct is most easily misunderstood. In fact, it is stronger and more important than instinct. I can't think of a better name, so I might as well call it aerial flying spirituality. For example, a pilot has many sophisticated instruments installed in front of him that can tell his plane where to fly and in what direction. As for these carrier pigeons, it is as if they have this kind of instrument installed in their brains, telling them how to fly even more brilliantly than instruments. Because they are not flying blindly, but navigating in the air. When they encounter storms and rain, they can avoid the storm and rain areas to the left or right and fly around them, and then resume their original route forward. However, why they can fly back to their destination, I can't explain, I'm afraid no one knows. However, it is probably related to their ears. Because if their ears are blocked, they cannot fly back, which is really a strange thing." According to Mr. Ross, carrier pigeons are not only very important in wartime, but also useful in peacetime. He believes that passenger and mail-carrying aircraft should carry one or two carrier pigeons on each flight to send messages for help in case the aircraft encounters danger, so that rescue can be obtained immediately.

Carrier pigeons have high intelligence and great courage. When they encounter eagles, they know how to avoid them, and they fly faster than eagles. They can also endure long flights. In the United States, the longest record created by a carrier pigeon is from Texas in the southwest to Maine in the northeast, a total of 2,150 miles, with an average speed of 700 miles per day. This was created by daytime-flying carrier pigeons. If the newly invented night-flying carrier pigeons are used, of course it will be even more than that.

The process of inventing and training these night flyers is extremely interesting and unique. The initial experiments began as early as ten years ago. In 1925, the Army Signal Corps stationed in the Monmouth base area specially selected ten pairs of the most ingenious and intelligent species from several species of experienced daytime carrier pigeons. During the day, these ten pairs of pigeons were always confined in cages. When dusk approached, these twenty birds were taken to a place not far from their original residence and released to allow them to try to fly back to their original place. This method of training continued, and gradually the time was changed later and the distance from the original place was slowly increased. Finally, they were able to fly back from a mile away in the dark.

These ten pairs of trained carrier pigeons were used as the basis to allow them to reproduce. Each generation of pigeons was trained. By the eighth generation of pigeons, they actually had the characteristic of flying at night from birth. With considerable training, they became the current night-flying carrier pigeons. Training begins on the eighteenth day after the pigeons hatch from the eggs. As dusk approaches, the young birds are released from the cage, allowing them to stand on the perching boards to observe their original environment and become familiar with the geographical situation. After a few days, they began to practice flying. In the dim twilight, they are taken to a place 200 yards away and released for their first return flight. Gradually, after a week, these birds' nocturnal flying characteristics become apparent, and they can fly back from a mile away in the dark. From then on, the distance is increased by a quarter of a mile every night. Later, it was increased to a dozen miles or even dozens of miles. After the training is successful, they are divided into three categories according to the most reliable flying distance at night: 5-mile pigeons, 10-mile pigeons, or 15-mile pigeons, for application.

The flying speed of night-flying carrier pigeons is also not much different from the speed of daytime-flying carrier pigeons. Depending on the climate and wind direction, it is usually 50 to 55 miles per hour. The letter bags they carry now have also been improved. They are not tied to the pigeon's legs, but are tied to the chest in a streamlined shape, which greatly reduces the wind resistance during flight. Therefore, each carrier pigeon can carry three ounces of mail. This is really a great help for military affairs.

Letter from Xiong Xiling

To the esteemed editor: I recently saw in the Tianjin special dispatch published in your newspaper on the 7th that Luo Jiaheng resigned and is ill in Tianjin, and that Song Zheyuan summoned Xiong Xiling to Tianjin on the 6th, and showed him certain instructions, etc. Xiling lives in seclusion in Shanghai and is unaware of worldly affairs. Shantou Kakuta Incident: Japanese Consul Suddenly Makes Demands

The two sides are still in negotiations

Shantou Dispatch: Since the Japanese Kakuta died violently in Shantou, the Japanese initially insisted that it was done by the Chinese and raised serious protests. After our side investigated the situation and protested, the Japanese could not find any excuse after several negotiations. Although this case has not been concluded, it has long since subsided. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, Wada, the commander of the Japanese Mako Port Fortress, arrived in Shantou on the "Akikaze" warship. The Japanese consul in Shantou, Harada, first sent a formal letter to the Shantou Municipal Government on the afternoon of the 1st, making demands regarding the Kakuta case and setting a deadline of 2 PM on the 2nd for a satisfactory response. His demands included tens of thousands of yuan in compensation for Kakuta's death, and other conditions, and he declared that if a satisfactory response was not received by the deadline, he would take independent action. The Shantou Municipal Government immediately telegraphed the province for instructions and received a reply, instructing them to resolve the matter properly. The Municipal Government then sent Councilor Huang to meet with the Japanese consul on the afternoon of the 2nd, replying to his demands that they needed to discuss them in detail to find a solution, and at the same time, secretly ordered all parties to be on alert. The people of Shantou could not help but feel anxious. Later, coincidentally, the commander of the Japanese Tenth Fleet, Nishioka Shigetai, arrived in Shantou, and also met with Mayor Chen at the Municipal Government at 8 PM on the 2nd, and more rumors spread in the market. Later, it was heard that Nishioka was willing to mediate in this case in a personal capacity, and the matter seemed to ease temporarily, so the people in the market also calmed down slightly. As for the resolution of this case, it is reported that the two sides are still in negotiations. (May 3rd)

Compatriots Anonymously Stow Away to Siam: Over Eight Hundred People Imprisoned

Siamese-Chinese Chamber of Commerce Replies to Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission; Unscrupulous Merchants Plan to Prevent Imprisoned Overseas Chinese from Returning Home; Shantou Municipal Government Summons Innkeepers

Shantou Dispatch: After a certain ship traveling between Shantou and Siam colluded with unscrupulous merchants to transport a large number of overseas Chinese stowaways to Siam and were apprehended, appeals were made from all sides to rescue them and to severely punish the culprits who arranged the stowaways. However, three months have passed since the incident, and the so-called culprits who arranged the stowaways have not been caught, nor have the imprisoned people received adequate rescue. Therefore, this case has gradually tended to subside. Now, the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Siam has listed the names, ages, native places, etc. of the Chinese overseas Chinese who were imprisoned in Siam and sent them to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. It is estimated that a total of more than 800 people were apprehended before and after. As for how the stowaways were arranged, it was mostly done by a certain inn, but no reply was received. Now that the date of release is approaching, the association, in addition to requesting the Siamese authorities to allow a reduction in the residence tax to be paid when each imprisoned person is released, has also sent letters to the relatives and friends of the imprisoned people in Siam to inquire whether they can raise the money to pay the tax on their behalf to ensure their residence, or the association will provide a certain amount of travel expenses to send them back to China. However, it is heard that all those who arranged the stowaways are carrying out activities to encourage the imprisoned overseas Chinese to pay a certain amount of tax on their release in order to prevent them from returning home, in the hope that this case can be resolved invisibly.

The Shantou Municipal Government received a report from the Siamese Chinese General Chamber of Commerce to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, stating that the association had investigated in Siam and found that as many as 800 Chinese overseas Chinese had been arrested and imprisoned by the Siamese government for more than three months (sentenced to 100 days of hard labor), and decided that if they were released after the term of imprisonment and no one in Siam would guarantee them and pay their personal tax on their behalf, they would be deported. More than 30 passengers who were escorted back from Jiangsu and Sharina last month. The Municipal Government immediately summoned them once to thoroughly investigate how they were deceived, and which inns and people handled the arrangements, so as to investigate them one by one, so that the handlers could return the original funds and compensate for the losses. Although the Municipal Government has obtained information, it has not yet determined how to punish them because the matter is too important. Recently, the Overseas Chinese Mutual Aid Society received telegrams from the Malaysian Chaozhou Association Federation, the Singapore Tongde Newspaper Society, the Singapore Teochew Association, the Dutch Sampoerna Teochew Association, and the Goat Mouth Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, requesting that they be immediately forwarded to the government, advocating for the thorough and strict handling of unscrupulous merchants and the officials responsible for checking the outgoing passengers when the ship sailed. 　Another passenger who was escorted back, Chen Yichun, complained to the Overseas Chinese Mutual Aid Society, stating that he was lured and defrauded of 95 silver dollars by the Nancheng Yingji Inn and innkeeper Chen Yayue on the day he was deceived. After Nancheng Yingji received the money, they promised to arrange transportation to and from and a safe landing, gave him a receipt for "tea money", sent him to a certain ship, and ordered him to hide in the bottom of the hold, declaring that if he could not land and was escorted back, the original money would be returned. Now he has suffered hardship in vain and has been escorted back to Shantou, and requested that the Municipal Government summon Chen Yayue and others from Nancheng Yingji to recover the original money. The Municipal Government recently summoned both parties to court based on this. Chen Yayue, the innkeeper of Nancheng Yingji, directly confessed that he had arranged for passengers to go to Siam. The Municipal Government transferred the case to the Shantou Court for handling on the grounds that Nancheng Inn had the crime of deliberately deceiving overseas Chinese to seek money. (May 2nd)

Guangdong Province: Ling Shan Earthquake Still Ongoing

County Residents Deeply Concerned About the Entire County Submerging, Request Dispatch of Geological Experts for Investigation

Guangzhou dispatch: A severe earthquake occurred in Lingshan County, southern Guangdong Province. The extent of the disaster was reported previously. According to a recent telegram from the county, tremors are still being felt in various parts of the county. Considering the earthquake disasters since April 1st, residents of the county have witnessed many villages being leveled or the ground sinking into deep pools. They are deeply concerned that the entire county may be submerged. County Magistrate Song Depei has specially submitted a petition to the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government, requesting immediate relief and the dispatch of experts to the county to investigate the geology, clarify the situation, and reassure the people. The original petition states: "The Lingshan Earthquake Disaster Area Refugee Relief Committee General Affairs Section, represented by Ye Fuqing and others, has submitted a report. Now, we have received the proposal from committee member Chen Buxiu on April 20th of this year, stating: 'We have found that since the first day of this month, our county has suddenly suffered from an earthquake disaster, and the entire county has been affected. The second and third districts have been particularly severely affected. The areas with drastic changes have become rubble fields, with numerous casualties, a heartbreaking sight. Currently, the disaster-stricken people are everywhere, crying out in distress, and the rumbling sounds still occur several times a day. Land subsidence and house collapses are still frequently heard. Therefore, people are panicked, feeling like a lonely city at sunset, precarious and uneasy. In this extraordinary situation, everything is at a standstill. Although we are fortunate to have generous and righteous gentlemen who are actively raising funds and providing relief, the disaster continues unabated, and the tremors are frequent. It is difficult to predict how this will end. Without a scientific analysis, it will be impossible to dispel rumors. Moreover, as the spring plowing season is approaching, if rural residents cannot be quickly reassured and return to their work, the losses will be even more unimaginable. Based on the above reasons, we hereby submit this proposal, earnestly requesting that the county government be instructed to telegraph the Guangdong Provincial Government, urging them to promptly dispatch geological experts to the county to conduct on-site investigations to determine the causes and consequences of the disaster, to calm the people's hearts, and to discuss a comprehensive relief plan, so that the people may rely on it. This is feasible, and we respectfully request a public decision.' This is approved and should be implemented. We hereby prepare this document and submit it to your office for review and approval for forwarding, to fulfill our public duty." We have found that a severe earthquake occurred in our county on [date], and there have been collapses of houses and deaths in the second and third districts, relatively many. The disaster is particularly severe. We have already reported this to you by telegram for your review and have personally led surgeons to provide relief, resettle refugees, and convene meetings with people from all walks of life to establish the Lingshan County Earthquake Disaster Area Refugee Relief Committee to investigate the disaster and discuss relief matters. As of today, the second and third districts are still experiencing earthquakes from time to time, and the disaster shows no sign of ending. The people are frightened, which is indeed the actual situation. According to the report, in addition to reporting the disaster of collapsed houses and dead livestock after the investigation is completed in the future, we hereby telegraph to request that you review and approve the transfer of the report to the Provincial Government to promptly dispatch geological experts to the county for investigation to clarify the truth and reassure the people. This is what we earnestly pray for. Respectfully, Song Depei, County Magistrate of Lingshan." (May 3rd)

Qingdao Municipal Government Employees Donate Salaries to Celebrate Birthday

All Departments Follow Suit

Qingdao dispatch: The Qingdao Municipal Government previously received letters and telegrams from the China Aviation Association and the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, stating that it is imperative to raise funds to purchase aircraft as a gift to celebrate Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday this year, in order to celebrate and promote national prestige. A method for municipal government employees to donate salaries and raise funds was specially drafted, and the first section of the Municipal Government Secretariat notified all departments and municipal and township district offices to implement it. The following is a transcript: "Qingdao Municipal Government Notice: 'To whom it may concern, we previously received letters and telegrams from the General Headquarters of the China Aviation Association and the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, stating that this year marks Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday, and provincial and municipal aviation association branches should urgently raise funds to purchase aircraft to celebrate the occasion and achieve the goal of national aviation salvation. We have been instructed to investigate and implement this matter. The municipal government has drafted a method for municipal government employees to donate salaries and raise funds, which is listed on a separate sheet, along with the original letters and telegrams. We hereby send this notice, hoping that you will investigate and implement it accordingly.'" Method of salary donation: The method for municipal government employees to donate salaries: 1. Those earning less than 30 yuan per month will have 0.3 yuan deducted monthly. 2. Those earning 31 to 50 yuan will have 0.6 yuan deducted monthly. 3. Those earning 51 to 100 yuan will have 3% deducted monthly. 4. Those earning 101 to 200 yuan will have 6% deducted monthly. 5. Those earning 201 to 300 yuan will have 8% deducted monthly. 6. Those earning more than 300 yuan will have 10% deducted monthly. The above method will be limited to three months. The salary donation ratios for the capital: A. Those earning 49 yuan or less will donate 2%. B. Those earning 50 to 99 yuan will donate 6%. C. Those earning 100 to 299 yuan will donate 7%. D. Those earning 300 to 399 yuan will donate 8%. E. Those earning 400 to 499 yuan will donate 9%. F. Those earning 500 yuan or more will donate 10%. Those with special office expenses must also donate according to the above percentages, all for a period of two months. (May 5th)

Miscellaneous Writings on Rural Hubei

(Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Cheng Jun)

Lewd Operas and Shrines in Daye

On the afternoon of April 3rd, I traveled from Yangxin to Daye by car. The distance between Yangxin and Daye is ninety li. I passed through Ditianqiao, Baishapu, and Xiaojipu, all of which belong to Yangxin. I got off the bus at the foot of Hailuo Mountain, which is only a lake away from the Daye county seat and still within Yangxin territory. The lake is called Jin Lake, which is formed by the convergence of spring water from the surrounding mountains. I hired a small boat and crossed it. The spring water was green, the setting sun cast shadows on the trees, and I leisurely floated in the middle of the lake, enjoying the scenery. The Daye county seat is surrounded by water on three sides, with no city walls and no soldiers checking. I went ashore and checked into the Daye Hotel. In recent days, I have traveled all over the disaster area. All I have seen are dilapidated houses with broken tiles and crumbling walls, or disaster victims with haggard faces. It is extremely troublesome to have soldiers checking luggage. Now I can finally relax a little. The streets of the county seat are long and stretch for three or four li. In the year 19 [of the Republic of China], it was captured by the Red Bandits three times. The commerce is extremely sluggish now. The county government's original office was burned down by the bandits and razed to the ground. It is now located in the Jin Lake Academy in the city center, which is very cramped. When I arrived at the county seat, the new and old county magistrates had just handed over. The people missed the old magistrate, Mr. Wu, quite a bit, presumably because he had good policies for the people. After the new magistrate, Mr. Cao, took office, he immediately went to Beijing for training, and the political affairs were handled by Secretary Yuan. I went to visit, waited for two hours, but the gatekeeper would not let me in. Later, I learned that he was out drinking and was acting like a typical official. I smiled and dismissed it and did not go again.

The area of the county is not as large as Yangxin. It was originally divided into ten districts, but now it has been reorganized into four district offices. There are many interconnected lakes and rivers, and the mountains undulate. Huangshigang and Shihuiyao are famous commercial and industrial areas. Most of the land in each village is used for growing crops rather than paddy fields. The rice produced can only feed the people for four months, and sweet potatoes can feed them for eight months, the same as in Yangxin. Fertile land is worth 100 yuan per mu, but now it has been reduced to 30 yuan. Barren land is only worth a few yuan. From the autumn of the 18th year [of the Republic of China] to the summer of the 21st year [of the Republic of China], the period of the most severe banditry, the entire county was communized. The fifth and sixth districts suffered the most, with approximately over ten thousand people killed by the bandits. Many houses were also destroyed, but the extent of destruction in the rural areas was not as severe as in Yangxin. The main force of the Red Bandits was wiped out by Chen Jicheng's troops last autumn. The search and suppression of scattered bandits was mostly carried out by armed anti-communist volunteer teams, as the people are strong and able to defend themselves. Among the villagers, there was a man named Zuo Hongde, who had fought fiercely with the bandits four or five hundred times and captured hundreds of bandit rifles. Currently, Longjiao Mountain in Yangxin, Nantantou and Huangmao Village in Echeng, and Huarushu, Longquanyang, Sanjiashan, and Luobeikou on the border between Yangxin and Daye are still harassed by scattered bandits. However, more than a hundred blockhouses have been built throughout the county, making it difficult for them to invade the interior.

In the 23rd and 24th years [of the Republic of China], the county suffered from repeated floods and droughts. The people's burden was heavy, and their lives were difficult. The land tax used to be as high as ten yuan per mu, but now it is calculated based on the price of unprocessed rice. One dan of rice is equivalent to two dan of land, and the tax is nine yuan and four fen per dan of rice, which is equivalent to five jiao per mu at the current price. The cost of Baojia [local self-governance system] depends on the number of Lianbao [joint defense unit] holding rifles and volunteer teams. Without a rifle-holding volunteer team, it costs no more than five yuan per month per Bao. With a rifle-holding volunteer team, it often costs more than ten yuan. The people feel most pained by the persistent abuses of the grain scribes, as the power to collect grain is still in the hands of the grain scribes. When collecting grain, they freely send people to the countryside to squeeze as much as possible, and the amount of excess collection often exceeds twice the amount that should be paid.

The people are naturally simple and litigious, often filing frivolous lawsuits. The so-called frivolous lawsuits are lawsuits filed even without a reason, as if they came out of nowhere. Since the opening of the coal and iron mines, the simple customs have changed to extravagance and licentiousness due to the convenience of transportation. The number of vagrants has been increasing day by day. Opium and gambling are rampant, and the government cannot prohibit them. The Huaguxi opera is the most corrupting of customs. Currently, in the new fourth district, two Huaguxi opera troupes are performing at the same time, and they have not stopped yet. Not only are local men and women flocking to it, but even the district chief is going to watch the opera and give "dacai" [tips]. (Giving "dacai" is like reporting the addition of an official, but without its formality. The female performers on the stage publicly call the person giving "dacai" "dear father," and he must give them money. It is extremely ugly.) District Chief Yi Yanfan is a victim of the May 30th incident in Yangxin. When the opera is being performed, gamblers are rampant. On stage, they are joking and laughing, while off stage, they are yelling and gambling. The district is adjacent to the bandit areas of Huarushu and Bajiaoting. Not only is it corrupting customs, but it is also likely to affect public security. Although the county magistrate has issued a strict ban, it is still regarded as a mere formality, probably because they have something to rely on.

There are also the so-called shrines, which are the greatest hidden worry in society. The people of Daye are extremely superstitious, and local ruffians take advantage of this psychology to set up shrines everywhere in the name of treating diseases and praying for blessings, secretly recruiting followers. People follow them as if going to market. Their potential power has now spread throughout the territory. The largest of the shrines are the "Western Heaven Different Gate," the "Big Knife Society," the "Tongshan Society," the "Doumu Altar," and the "Luo Zhenren Altar." The so-called "Western Heaven Different Gate" resembles the Golden Light Sect in the east. The "Big Knife Society" and others are remnants of the White Lotus Sect, the Red Lantern Society, and the Boxer Rebellion. Each type has titles such as "Pen Holder," "Great Teacher," "Great Guide," and "Assistant." The "Pen Holder" is said to have a god attached to his body and has the highest position and the greatest power. The "Great Teacher" and "Great Guide" make decisions, and the "Assistant" also makes decisions. All those below the Teacher are responsible for preaching and guiding. The followers use a red circle with a double circle inside as a symbol, write the Heavenly Fortune year, and do not recognize the Republic of China's official calendar. It is heard that these strange organizations are unified under the so-called "Ten Thousand Sects Society" and receive its guidance. People only blindly follow out of superstition, but those in charge are not only aiming to accumulate wealth and bewilder the masses. Therefore, those who know the inside story cannot help but feel chilled.

Suzhou: Representatives of North China Yarn Mills Go to Wuxi

The seven major yarn mills in North China, Henan, Shanxi and other provinces, including Yufeng, have formed the North China Yarn Mill Association to improve the industry. They have sent Yan Qingxiang, Zai Wenxin, Liu Chijun and other twenty people as representatives to form a delegation to go south for inspection. They first went to Shanghai to visit various yarn mills, and then came to Suzhou from Shanghai on the 6th to visit Suzhou Lun Yarn Mill, Huasheng Paper Plate Factory and other major factories. The Wuxian Industrial Branch held a welcome meeting and a public banquet. The delegation left Suzhou for Wuxi yesterday morning (7th) to visit.

Rent Riot Comes to an End

In the rural areas of Suzhou, such as Chefang and Xietang, farmers have repeatedly launched major rent riots, citing poor harvests. Police teams and villagers clashed, but fortunately, the authorities sent teams to suppress them, and the riot came to an end. However, this riot was caused by the authorities sending personnel to collect rent. Although the riot has subsided, rent collection is still in its early stages, and it seems that it cannot be simply ended with suppression. Therefore, rent collection committee members Zhang Qianli and others submitted four methods to the county government for approval: 1. Tenant farmers must pay their rent arrears at the designated grain depot by May 21st. After the deadline, the county will send security teams to collect rent from door to door. 2. The price discount will be calculated as seven yuan before the 7th, seven yuan and fifteen fen before the 14th, and seven yuan and thirty fen before the 21st. After the deadline, it will be calculated as seven yuan and forty-five fen. 3. Those who pay within the 21st will receive an additional discount. 4. Those who are truly poor will have their village and township Baojia leaders prove it and issue a debt note for future payment. The above methods have been approved by County Magistrate Deng, and the grain depot owners have no objections. They will be implemented immediately, and the farmers in each village also consider them fair. Therefore, they have been paying rent in succession, and there should be no other problems. County Magistrate Deng, in response to the farmers in Lu Tomb and Yangshang Villages gathering to resist rent, yesterday (7th) specially instructed the Public Security Bureau to quickly investigate and secretly arrest them, and instructed the police district in charge to handle it carefully.

Extension of Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway Opening

After the completion of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway Jinlu project, test runs have been carried out twice with excellent results. Currently, they are rushing to paint the station houses along the route, which is expected to be completed within a month. As for the official opening date, it was originally scheduled for July 1st, but according to news from transportation circles, it will be postponed to July 15th for the official opening to transport goods. The opening to passenger trains will still take time, as the equipment and procedures are not yet ready. It is heard that the railway police affairs will be handled concurrently by the South Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, and the train affairs will be handled concurrently by the Hangzhou Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway.

Murder Case Due to Adultery Occurs Outside Changmen

Cao Rengen, who lives outside the South Gate of Wuxi, recently learned that his wife, Cao Zhang, and her lover, Zhao Baomai, were hiding in Suzhou. He immediately came to Suzhou with his friend Zhang Yifengshan to inquire with Zhang Yisan at 41 Damalu outside Changmen. Zhang Yisan kept Cao Rengen at his home on the evening of the 6th. On the one hand, he went out with Zhang Fengshan under the pretext of looking for Cao Zhang and Zhao Yinbao. Zhang Yisan induced Zhang Fengshan to a remote place north of the Main Lord Temple near the train station. Zhao Yinbao suddenly flashed out from the roadside, along with two other accomplices. Zhao Yinbao grabbed Zhang Yanshan, pushed him to the ground, and untied a black belt, cutting and strangling Zhang Fengshan's neck, intending to strangle Zhang Fengshan to death. At that time, Zhang Fengshan fainted. Zhao Yinbao and others thought that he was dead and immediately dispersed. Fortunately, Zhang Fengshan's fate was not to die. The black belt suddenly broke, and he gradually woke up. It was already 2 a.m. Because he could not walk, he crawled to the vicinity of Guangji Bridge on Shantang Street and reported to the police officer on duty. The police officer took him to the police district in charge and sent police to Zhang Yisan's home. Because Zhang Yisan was not there, his wife was interrogated. It was learned that Zhang Yisan, Cao Zhang, and others were staying at the Renhe Public Inn in Yangjiayuanzi Lane. The police went to the Renhe Public Inn and arrested Zhang Yisan, Cao Zhang, and others, along with the tea boy Huang Zhaojin. On the evening of the 6th, an accomplice named Jin Xiaocheng was also arrested and taken to the branch station. On the 7th, they were sent to the Public Security Bureau. After Zhang, the section chief, interrogated them, he transferred them to the local court for strict handling. The Public Security Bureau sent police to strictly arrest Zhao Yinbao and bring him to justice. However, Cao Rengen suddenly disappeared, and the authorities are investigating whether he was murdered.

Wuxi: Mr. Etman Comes to Wuxi to Inspect Labor

Mr. Etman, Overseas Director of the International Labor Bureau, came to China to investigate labor conditions. At 8:34 p.m. on the 6th, accompanied by his wife and Cheng Haifeng, Director of the International Labor China Branch, he arrived in Wuxi from Nanjing. Gao Jian, President of the Provincial Education Institute of Wuxi, had been notified in advance by the Ministry of Industry and specially accompanied local business leaders Rong Desheng, Cheng Jingtang, Hua Shaochun and others to meet him at the station. Mr. Etman, accompanied by Mr. Cheng Haifeng, visited the Shenxin Third Factory and the Maoxin First Factory. In the afternoon, he visited the Qingfeng Yarn Factory and the Luxin Textile Dyeing Factory and will visit Huaxin Yongtai and other silk factories today to investigate labor conditions. He will stay for about three or four days and then go to Shanghai.

Special Commissioner's Office Plans to Establish a Factory for Opium Addicts

Zang Qifang, the Special Commissioner of the Wuxi District Administrative Inspectorate, has repeatedly received reports from various counties stating that during this period of strict drug prohibition, after the expiration of the general reporting period, the number of opium offenders has increased sharply, and it is almost impossible to accommodate those who should be sent to drug rehabilitation centers. They requested that the detention centers be expanded to accommodate opium offenders. The Special Commissioner believes that expanding the detention centers would be very costly, and it would be difficult to find suitable housing. He intends to convert the detention centers into factories for opium addicts, so that the offenders can have the opportunity to learn skills and make a living independently in the future. He has prepared a plan and submitted it to the Civil Affairs Department for approval. The factory site is planned to be established in Wuxian, divided into weaving, sewing, dyeing, textile, daily necessities, and chemical crafts departments. All opium addicts under the age of 50 must be admitted to the factory to learn skills for a limited period of six months. At the same time, they will be given academic and military training. Each period will have a limit of 500 people. Those with excellent skills will be given prizes to encourage them. It is heard that the initial funding is estimated to be over 31,000 yuan, and the annual recurring expenses after opening will be over 30,000 yuan. Once approved by the Civil Affairs Department, preparations will begin immediately.

Robbery and Assault Case Occurs in the Sixth District

Chen Zongshun, a resident of Nanchen Lane, Group 5, Jia 8, Maijiu Lane Village, Sixth District of this county, is 56 years old. He has been a farmer for generations and is still able to make a living. Last year's autumn harvest was abundant, and he accumulated hundreds of dan of grain. This spring, the price of rice rose, so he sold his stored grain and obtained over a thousand yuan, which he stored at home, attracting the covetous eyes of bandits. At midnight the other day, about thirty bandits suddenly broke into his house. They spoke the local dialect and each held flashlights, guns, and iron rulers. They broke down the door and tied up all the members of Zongshun's family with ropes, threatening them not to make a sound. They then ransacked the house and searched through all the boxes and cabinets. All the rice money was stolen. Zongshun and his wife were also severely beaten. Yesterday, they reported the robbery to the district office and requested that it be forwarded to the county government to investigate and recover the stolen goods.

Yinjiang Qingyang Red Pill Case Sent to the Province for Interrogation

Huang Gonghe Cocoon Firm in Qingyang Town, Sixth District, secretly established a red pill manufacturing organization the year before last. It was uncovered by Wu Bingjun, the former head of the Second Public Security Branch. However, because of bribery in Wuxi, the case was dismissed. This case involves many people and has not been closed. Recently, someone reported it to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters. Yesterday (6th), County Magistrate Yuan ordered the police to go to Qingyang and arrest Xu Zukun, Jiang Hong, Zhu Hongji, and Zang Xihong and take them to the county. They will be sent to the Garrison Headquarters for interrogation.

Haimen: Songji Port Shipping Boat Robbed

In recent years, this county has been unsettled, and robberies have suddenly become rampant. Songji Port and a corner of Songhai Road are particularly frequented by bandits. Passengers going back and forth are often robbed, and boat accidents occur from time to time. Therefore, travelers regard this port as a dangerous place. The other morning, during a small flood, the passengers on the wheel could not enter the port after unloading their sculls, so they floated in the river. They beckoned the shipping boats to ferry the passengers and luggage in batches. Unexpectedly, as the ship was loading passengers and starting the engine, a bandit boat suddenly came from afar, approached the shipping boat, and more than a dozen burly men jumped out, holding sharp weapons and threatening them not to make a sound. All passengers were robbed by bandits. They took the Beijing Special Trust

The "Food" Problem in Beiping

— Special Dispatch from Beiping

According to recent statistics, the population of Beiping is 1,574,582. This does not include the 3,122 foreigners and those living in the embassy area of the Dongjiaominxiang. Among Chinese cities, aside from Shanghai, this is probably the most populous. The "food" problem for such a large number of people is, of course, a matter worthy of attention. The situation in several aspects is outlined below.

From the perspective of daily necessities for family life, general prices in Beiping are actually a bit cheaper than elsewhere. For example, regarding flour, the current market price for Fuxing brand is 3 yuan 6 jiao 6 fen per bag, Pao Che brand is 3 yuan 5 jiao 6 fen per bag, Tianjin rice is 1 jiao 05 fen per jin, Saigon rice is 1 jiao per jin, and Wuxi rice is 13 yuan 4 jiao per shi. These cannot be considered cheap, but the prices of the following raw materials, which have a closer relationship with the lives of ordinary citizens, are relatively cheaper. For example, millet is 6 fen 5 li per jin, corn flour (i.e., maize flour) is 4 fen 5 li per jin, millet flour is 4 fen 8 li per jin, beef is 1 jiao 7 fen per jin, mutton is 2 jiao 4 fen per jin, pork is 2 jiao per jin, spinach is 12 "mei" per jin, rapeseed is 40 "mei" per jin, cilantro is 48 "mei" per jin, chives are 28 "mei" per jin, celery is 32 "mei" per jin, and small radishes are 6 "mei" per bunch. (In Beiping, large copper coins are used, each called "two mei." "Twelve mei" means six large copper coins, which, at the current market price, is equivalent to one small copper coin plus one-third in the Beijing-Shanghai area). Such cheap prices are not available in other cities.

For general upper-middle-class families, the main food sources are rice, flour, beef, mutton, pork, and various vegetables. For lower-class families, the main food sources are millet, millet flour, corn flour, and various vegetables. In addition, for coal, oil, salt, and other items needed for cooking, according to market prices, raw coal is 3 jiao 3 fen per 100 jin, hard coal is 4 jiao 5 fen per 100 jin, sesame oil (i.e., sesame seed oil) is 8 "mei" per liang, peanut oil is 7 "mei" per liang, and salt is 80 "mei" per jin.

Under normal circumstances, upper-middle-class families spend at least half as much on "food" as in the Beijing-Shanghai area. Spending 200 to 100 yuan a month in this regard is considered top-tier, while 80 to 50 yuan is considered middle-tier (small families with fewer than five people spend even less). As for lower-class families, one mao per person per day is enough to eat.

The economic situation for common people's food is so bad that people who can't even organize a family have to live this "commoner" life. This "commoner" life means having a meal or not, earning more and eating more, earning less and eating less, and not earning and not eating. Eating one meal a day is common. When they earn money, they immediately buy ready-made food on the street, eat to gain strength, and then go back to earning. (Their entire lives consist of only these two things.) The main foods are sesame cakes, fried dough sticks (similar to youtiao in the South), fried tofu, steamed buns, wotou (made from corn flour), roasted sweet potatoes, etc. If they want soup, there's wonton for three large "mei" a bowl or douzhi for five large "mei" a bowl. Cutting some sauce (pork, donkey, beef, etc.) for ten large "mei" to make a side dish is considered a very rich meal.

Usually, a person spends about twenty "mei" per meal. Spending more than one mao per meal is rare for them. People living this kind of life are mostly rickshaw pullers, children who pick up trash, and old women who exchange lamp wicks (i.e., matches) for scrap paper. Therefore, when you are surrounded by more than a dozen pairs of rickshaw pullers with longing eyes, crying to you, "Sir, Sir, I haven't eaten anything all day," or when you hand a pile of old newspapers to the old women who exchange lamp wicks, and they tremble their withered hands, only willing to give you a box of red-headed matches, while pleadingly muttering, "Sir, please give me enough to buy another wotou," these are all true situations and not just business tactics.

Restaurants: The number of restaurants in Beiping is probably unimaginable to people living in the South. It's not an exaggeration to describe the situation as "lined up in rows." A large population is the first reason. Everyone lives a relaxed life, so they have leisure to be particular about this, which is the second reason. There are not many entertainment options, so they have to treat eating out as a form of entertainment, which is the third reason.

Classified, they can be roughly divided into four categories: Western restaurants, banquet restaurants, snack restaurants, and food shops. Eating Western food is not common in Beiping, and there are only eleven restaurants. The most famous is the Jieying Western Restaurant on Langfang Toutiao. Usually, you can get a meal for 1.5 to 2.8 yuan. Banquet restaurants are divided into Shandong restaurants, Huaiyang restaurants, Guizhou restaurants, Henan restaurants, Guangdong restaurants, Sichuan restaurants, and mutton restaurants, etc. Each of these has its own characteristics and famous representative restaurants, such as Dongxinglou for Shandong cuisine, Lumingchun for Huaiyang cuisine, Xiqianyang for Guizhou cuisine, Donglaishun for mutton cuisine, Rongyuan for Henan cuisine, Donghualou for Guangdong cuisine, and Dalu Chun for Sichuan cuisine.

The number of snack restaurants is also countless. They have the flavor of banquet restaurants but are not as formal. A Beiping banquet costs about ten yuan, which is considered average. In a snack restaurant, drinking with two or three people costs only three or four yuan. As for food shops, they serve single dishes or provide board. A dish and a soup usually cost one to two mao. Board costs seven to nine yuan per month. Most of the patrons of these kinds of food shops are students. Because there are many students in Beiping, business is mostly very prosperous.

Special Foods: In addition, famous foods in Beiping, such as Peking roast duck from Quanjude and Bianyifang, roasted beef from the Wang family in Aner Hutong, sauced beef from Jushengzhai, sauced mutton from Yueshengqi, white stewed meat from Shaguoju, fried dough pieces from Mujiazhai, and fried triangles from Douchu, are famous foods that anyone who has ever "stayed" in Beiping, whether from the North or South, must try.

In summary, whether rich or poor, the food problem in Beiping is generally more comfortable and cheaper than elsewhere. A friend who used to do propaganda work once told me, "Beiping people are the most difficult people in China to be influenced by propaganda." Therefore, Beiping society is also relatively stagnant. However, in recent years, it has become poorer day by day. It's not that Beiping people can't endure. When they become so poor that even the minimum "commoner life" can't be maintained, perhaps this stagnant society will change a bit.

City Party Headquarters to Hold Memorial Meeting

According to the Guomin News Agency, tomorrow (the 9th) is National Humiliation Memorial Day, a day that commemorates the "May Seventh" incident when Japan issued the final ultimatum of the Twenty-One Demands, the "May Ninth" signing of the traitorous treaty by Yuan Shikai, the failure of the "August 29th" Opium War, the "September Seventh" signing of the Boxer Protocol, the "May Third" Jinan Massacre, the "May Thirtieth" Shanghai Massacre, and the "June 23rd" Shameen Massacre, among other national humiliations. Tea Reception

Chairman's Speech

After performing the formalities, Chairman Zhang Zilian first delivered a welcoming speech, stating briefly that the Party-State flag is a symbol representing the Party-State, and the central and local leaders have always paid attention to it. Since the establishment of our bureau under orders, with the guidance and supervision of the Central Party Headquarters and the Ministry of Interior, and the enthusiastic promotion of compatriots from all walks of life, the flag system has become increasingly unified, which has greatly benefited the awakening of national consciousness and the promotion of national spirit. Our bureau manufactures products according to the methods prescribed by the Central Government, with three characteristics: 1. Never fading; 2. Whole piece of fabric; 3. Domestic raw materials. After your visit today, you will be able to understand the manufacturing process. In the future, we hope that you will provide guidance to promote the national emblem and revitalize the national spirit.

Mr. Zhang's Report

Then, Committee Member of the Bureau and Manager of Shanghai Textile Printing and Dyeing Company Zhang Rongchu reported, stating briefly that the textile printing and dyeing industry in our country is very immature. The integration of these four aspects is rarely seen domestically. I have been striving for years to promote domestic goods and reduce leakages, and with the assistance of various parties, the scale is initially established. However, our country's industry is under the oppression of foreign goods, and business is difficult. Although our factory is somewhat comforting in terms of equipment and layout, we have experienced many hardships and difficulties. Manufacturing the Party-State flag is in line with the central government's and Party-State leaders' intention to rectify the flag system and with the encouragement of my friend Zhang Zilian, to serve the Party-State, not to make a profit. Today, your presence allows you to understand the manufacturing process of our factory, from spinning to weaving to printing to dyeing, from cotton to the completion of the Party-State flag and various products. We hope that you, gentlemen, will not hesitate to provide guidance and promote the national emblem and promote domestic goods, so that Rongchu can carry out his original intention and strive to maintain the national industry and the livelihood of workers. This is what I sincerely hope for.

Mayor's Speech

Then, Mayor Wu delivered a speech, briefly stating that today, the Party-State Flag Manufacturing and Sales Bureau welcomes guests from all walks of life to visit the manufacturing content of the Party-State flag and has earnestly provided hospitality. I am both grateful for the opportunity to visit and offer my thanks. The Party-State flag declares the truth of the country and symbolizes the nation. Therefore, the manufacturing of the Party-State flag must be taken seriously. The central government has given serious consideration to the manufacturing of the Party-State flag. In order to achieve uniformity and consistency, the Party-State Flag Manufacturing and Sales Bureau was specially organized to be in charge of the manufacturing and sales of the Party-State flag. Since the Party-State flag represents a country and embodies the spirit of a nation, the uniformity of the Party-State flag proves the completeness of a country in its organization, and the tidiness of the Party-State flag proves that a nation is disciplined and orderly. Now that the Party-State flag has a dedicated agency in charge of its manufacturing, it should not be difficult to achieve uniformity and tidiness. The Party-State flag is extremely important in the national significance, which should be known to all of us. However, in order to show our actions, we should have respect for the Party-State flag. Our respect for the Party-State flag is our respect for the country and the nation. This is what we must have a clear understanding of. If Chinese people can show respect for the Party-State flag, foreigners can also show respect for our country's Party-State flag. Therefore, in the future, we hope to work hard to ensure that every household should have a Party-State flag and that everyone should show respect for the Party-State flag. This represents the concentration of national importance and the fullness of patriotic spirit. In order to complete this mission, not only should the Party-State Flag Manufacturing and Sales Bureau work hard, but also people from all walks of life should work together to achieve the uniformity and tidiness of the Party-State flag and the goal of everyone having one and everyone respecting it.

Speeches from All Walks of Life

Then, Wang Xiaolai spoke, stating briefly that he was grateful for the bureau's diligent hospitality. Today, the factory manufactures uniform and tidy Party-State flags from the process of self-spinning, self-weaving, self-printing, and self-dyeing. After the visit, I felt something about national affairs. I believe that if our 400 million compatriots can all have the spirit of "self-love, love of country, love of people" and "self-rescue, saving the country, saving people" and work hard to move forward, then our country and nation will be able to coexist in glory with this bright and splendid Party-State flag. Then, Lin Kanghou spoke, stating briefly that the meeting place today is full of Party-State flags, with bright colors and tidy styles, which is inspiring. The Party-State flag is the facade of the Republic of China. If the facade is decorated with spirit and color, it can arouse the love and affection of the general public. Therefore, I hope that the people of the country will also pay attention to this facade of the Republic of China, and I especially hope that the Party-State Flag Manufacturing and Sales Bureau will work harder and not fail the central government's heavy responsibility for manufacturing. Li Dachao and others also gave speeches. The chairman's reply was omitted for brevity. Mayor Wu, Zhu Qinglan, Zhang Guoren, Hong Ruizhao, Li Dachao, Gui Yanfang, Pan Yangyao, and others also inscribed poems to leave as souvenirs.

Manufacturing Content

Guests arrived at the factory successively and were guided to visit various departments of the factory by staff assigned by the bureau. The factory is divided into five departments: 1. Spinning Department: spins cotton into cotton yarn, with 52 spinning wheels and 15,000 spindles. 2. Weaving Department: weaves cotton yarn into cloth, with 800 looms. 3. Bleaching Department: bleaches the cloth, with 6 bleaching machines. 4. Dyeing Department: dyes the bleached cloth with a base color first. 5. Printing Department: formally prints the colors of the Party-State flag on the dyed cloth, then washes it with steam. The raw materials used by the factory, except for pigments, are all domestic goods. There are more than 1,300 workers. The daily output can reach 200,000 flags for sizes one to three, 80,000 flags for size four, and more than 10,000 flags for sizes five and six. Flags of sizes seven, eight, nine, and ten are produced by a reasonable combination of machines and manual labor, with about 1,000 flags per day. The machines used are all the latest models from various countries, so production is faster and management is easier. Each Party-State flag, from cotton, must go through 46 procedures in its manufacturing process, which shows that success in everything is not easy.
